 media report ke mutabik NCERT ke deshbhar main paanch trennig centre hai, jahaan visheshgyon kaa team pre skulon ke liye paathyakram taiyaar karne main jute gai he
 In the month of June, a case of cutting about 16000 trees was reported in Delhi to build seven government colony, out of which a few thousand trees have been cut, after which the matter got hot and went to court
 sarkaar par dabaav bana to sarkaar ne ped kaatane kii manjuuri radd kii, court or engiti ne bhi ped kaatane par philhal roak laga di
 After that, the cutting of trees for those seven colonies was stopped, but apart from that, the work of cutting trees for large scale different projects in Delhi and around is going on continuously
 aise main agar sarkaar kuch paudhe un kaate gaye pedo ke baad laga de rahi he to bhi yah raahat kii khabar he
 In Delhi, fearless miscreants shot dead cashiers and guards in broad daylight and looted a cash van
 vine ke cash box main kareeb 12 lakh rupee maujuud the
 During this, the miscreants also fired about 20 rounds
 vaardaat ko anjaam dekar badmaash maukey se faraar ho gaye
 The miscreants committed this robbery incident outside the Bardhaman Mall of Narela
 us vaqt dopaher ke dhai baj rahe the
 Kikash Van, a private company, came to collect cash from a shop
 cash colect karne ke baad jaise hi kaisier rajnikant or guard prem kumaar paisa cash vine main rakh rahe the, tabhi achaanak 3 bike savaar badmaashon ne vahaan firing shuru kar di
 The miscreants fired about 15 bullets into the cashier's body and also shot 3 to 4 guards
 iske baad badmaash kareeb 12 lakh rupee se bharaa box lekar vahaan se faraar ho gaye
 The place where the incident was carried out, there was a crowd
 lekin goliyon kii aawaaj sunakar vahaan bhagdad si much gai
 Before leaving, the miscreants dropped the shutter of the shop from which the cash was collected
 badmaashon ke jane ke baad donon ghayalon ko hospital le jaaya gaya

 badmashone jis tarah se chand senkend main hi 20 round ke kareeb goli chalaai, isse saaf he ki unke paas atyaadhunik hathiyaar maujuud the

 You must be using Indian notes and coins every day, you must have learned a lot of tricks to check fake notes, yet there are many things related to rupees that you will not know about
 jaaniye bhartiya rupee or sikke sein sambandhit 10 khaas baaten:1
 Five thousand and ten thousand notes were in circulation from 1954 to 1978
 2
 After independence, Pakistan used to use Indian notes by stamping its country
 vahaan adhik noton ke print hone ke baad yah upyog band ho gaya
 3
 hindi or angreji bhashaa ke alaava noton par duusare kul 15 bhashaaon kaa istemaal hota he
 Kashmiri, Malayalam, Marathi, Oriya, Nepali, Punjabi, Sanskrit, Telugu, Urdu, Tamil, Kannada, Assamese, Konkani, Marathi, Gujarati and Bengali are used on the second note with Rs 10, 20 and 50 rupees
 4
 Coins of 5 rupees were smuggled into Bangladesh to make blades
 5 rupee ke sikke se 6 blade banaae jate the or prayek blade kii keemat 2 rupee thi
